follows this sequence:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eInformation Gap Recognition\u003c/strong\u003e: Roo identifies missing information needed to proceed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSpecific Question Creation\u003c/strong\u003e: Roo formulates a clear, targeted question\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSuggestion Development\u003c/strong\u003e: Roo creates relevant suggested answers (optional but recommended)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTool Invocation\u003c/strong\u003e: Assistant invokes the tool with question and optional suggestions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUI Presentation\u003c/strong\u003e: Question and suggestions are displayed to the user as interactive elements\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUser Response\u003c/strong\u003e: The user selects a suggestion or provides a custom answer\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMessage Handling\u003c/strong\u003e: System handles both partial and complete messages\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFor streaming responses, processes chunks as they arrive\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFor complete messages, processes the entire response at once\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMaintains state consistency regardless of message chunking\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eResponse Processing\u003c/strong\u003e: System wraps the response in \u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;answer\u0026gt;\u003c/code\u003e tags and preserves images\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eContext Integration\u003c/strong\u003e: Response is added to the conversation history\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTask Continuation\u003c/strong\u003e: Roo proceeds with the task using the new information\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eExamples When data-testid="more-file-actions-button" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 ffkqe prc-Button-ButtonBase-c50BI js-blob-dropdown-click fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">ask_followup_question</h1><a id="user-content-ask_followup_question" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: ask_followup_question" href="#ask_followup_question"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>ask_followup_question</code> tool enables interactive communication by asking specific questions to gather additional information needed to complete tasks effectively.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Parameters</h2><a id="user-content-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Parameters" href="#parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The tool accepts these parameters:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>question</code> (required): The specific question to ask the user</li>
<li><code>follow_up</code> (optional): A list of 2-4 suggested answers that help guide user responses, each within <code>&lt;suggest&gt;</code> tags</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What It Does</h2><a id="user-content-what-it-does" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What It Does" href="#what-it-does"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This tool creates a conversational interface between Roo and the user, allowing for gathering clarification, additional details, or user preferences when facing ambiguities or decision points. Each question can include suggested responses to streamline the interaction.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">When is it used?</h2><a id="user-content-when-is-it-used" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: When is it used?" href="#when-is-it-used"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>When critical information is missing from the original request</li>
<li>When Roo needs to choose between multiple valid implementation approaches</li>
<li>When technical details or preferences are required to proceed</li>
<li>When Roo encounters ambiguities that need resolution</li>
<li>When additional context would significantly improve the solution quality</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Features</h2><a id="user-content-key-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Features" href="#key-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Provides a structured way to gather specific information without breaking workflow</li>
<li>Includes suggested answers to reduce user typing and guide responses</li>
<li>Maintains conversation history and context across interactions</li>
<li>Supports responses containing images and code snippets</li>
<li>Available in all modes as part of the "always available" tool set</li>
<li>Enables direct user guidance on implementation decisions</li>
<li>Formats responses with <code>&lt;answer&gt;</code> tags to distinguish them from regular conversation</li>
<li>Resets consecutive error counter when used successfully</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Limitations</h2><a id="user-content-limitations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Limitations" href="#limitations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Limited to asking one specific question per tool use</li>
<li>Presents suggestions as selectable options in the UI</li>
<li>Cannot force structured responses  users can still respond freely</li>
<li>Excessive use can slow down task completion and create a fragmented experience</li>
<li>Suggested answers must be complete, with no placeholders requiring user edits</li>
<li>No built-in validation for user responses</li>
<li>Contains no mechanism to enforce specific answer formats</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How It Works</h2><a id="user-content-how-it-works" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How It Works" href="#how-it-works"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When the <code>ask_followup_question</code> tool is invoked, it follows this process:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Parameter Validation</strong>: Validates the required <code>question</code> parameter and checks for optional suggestions</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Ensures question text is provided</li>
<li>Parses any suggested answers from the <code>follow_up</code> parameter using the <code>fast-xml-parser</code> library</li>
<li>Normalizes suggestions into an array format even if there's only one suggestion</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>JSON Transformation</strong>: Converts the XML structure into a standardized JSON format for UI display</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  question: &quot;User's question here&quot;,
  suggest: [
    { answer: &quot;Suggestion 1&quot; },
    { answer: &quot;Suggestion 2&quot; }
  ]
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">question</span>: <span class="pl-s">"User's question here"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">suggest</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">answer</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Suggestion 1"</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">answer</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Suggestion 2"</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>UI Integration</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Passes the JSON structure to the UI layer via the <code>ask("followup", ...)</code> method</li>
<li>Displays selectable suggestion buttons to the user in the interface</li>
<li>Creates an interactive experience for selecting or typing a response</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Response Collection and Processing</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Captures user text input and any images included in the response</li>
<li>Wraps user responses in <code>&lt;answer&gt;</code> tags when returning to the assistant</li>
<li>Preserves any images included in the user's response</li>
<li>Maintains the conversational context by adding the response to the history</li>
<li>Resets the consecutive error counter when the tool is used successfully</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Error Handling</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Tracks consecutive mistakes using a counter</li>
<li>Resets the counter when the tool is used successfully</li>
<li>Provides specific error messages:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>For missing parameters: "Missing required parameter 'question'"</li>
<li>For XML parsing: "Failed to parse operations: [error message]"</li>
<li>For invalid format: "Invalid operations xml format"</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Contains safeguards to prevent tool execution when required parameters are missing</li>
<li>Increments consecutive mistake count when errors occur</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Workflow Sequence</h2><a id="user-content-workflow-sequence" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Workflow Sequence" href="#workflow-sequence"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The question-answer cycle follows this sequence:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Information Gap Recognition</strong>: Roo identifies missing information needed to proceed</li>
<li><strong>Specific Question Creation</strong>: Roo formulates a clear, targeted question</li>
<li><strong>Suggestion Development</strong>: Roo creates relevant suggested answers (optional but recommended)</li>
<li><strong>Tool Invocation</strong>: Assistant invokes the tool with question and optional suggestions</li>
<li><strong>UI Presentation</strong>: Question and suggestions are displayed to the user as interactive elements</li>
<li><strong>User Response</strong>: The user selects a suggestion or provides a custom answer</li>
<li><strong>Message Handling</strong>: System handles both partial and complete messages
<ul dir="auto">
<li>For streaming responses, processes chunks as they arrive</li>
<li>For complete messages, processes the entire response at once</li>
<li>Maintains state consistency regardless of message chunking</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Response Processing</strong>: System wraps the response in <code>&lt;answer&gt;</code> tags and preserves images</li>
<li><strong>Context Integration</strong>: Response is added to the conversation history</li>
<li><strong>Task Continuation</strong>: Roo proceeds with the task using the new information</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Examples When Used</h2><a id="user-content-examples-when-used" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Examples When Used" href="#examples-when-used"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>When developing a web application, Roo might ask about preferred styling frameworks (Bootstrap, Tailwind, custom CSS)</li>
<li>When creating an API, Roo might ask about authentication methods (JWT, OAuth, API keys)</li>
<li>When refactoring code, Roo might ask about prioritizing performance vs. readability</li>
<li>When setting up a database, Roo might ask about specific schema design preferences</li>
<li>When creating a custom feature, Roo might ask about specific behavior expectations</li>
<li>When troubleshooting errors, Roo might ask about specific environment details</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Response Format</h2><a id="user-content-response-format" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Response Format" href="#response-format"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When a user responds to a question, the response is formatted with <code>&lt;answer&gt;</code> tags for clarity and consistency. This format helps clearly separate the user's answer from other conversation elements.</p>
<p dir="auto">Example response format:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;answer&gt;
Use Tailwind CSS for utility-first styling with maximum flexibility
&lt;/answer&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>&lt;answer&gt;
Use Tailwind CSS for utility-first styling with maximum flexibility
&lt;/answer&gt;
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Key characteristics of the response format:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Surrounded by <code>&lt;answer&gt;</code> tags</li>
<li>Preserves formatting of the original response</li>
<li>Maintains images if included in the response</li>
<li>Returns the complete text, even for long responses</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage Examples</h2><a id="user-content-usage-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage Examples" href="#usage-examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Asking about implementation preferences:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;ask_followup_question&gt;

&lt;/follow_up&gt;
